--- src\pages\MySummaries.jsx ---

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { 
  MagnifyingGlassIcon, 
  FunnelIcon,
  DocumentTextIcon,
  CalendarIcon,
  ClockIcon,
  SparklesIcon
} from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';

// Custom SummaryCard component (built-in to match style)
const SummaryCard = ({ summary, onClick }) => {
  const getColorStyles = (title) => {
    if (title.includes('Machine')) return { gradient: 'from-blue-500 to-teal-500', bg: 'bg-blue-50', text: 'text-blue-600', border: 'border-blue-200' };
    if (title.includes('Data')) return { gradient: 'from-green-500 to-emerald-500', bg: 'bg-green-50', text: 'text-green-600', border: 'border-green-200' };
    if (title.includes('Database')) return { gradient: 'from-purple-500 to-pink-500', bg: 'bg-purple-50', text: 'text-purple-600', border: 'border-purple-200' };
    if (title.includes('Web')) return { gradient: 'from-orange-500 to-red-500', bg: 'bg-orange-50', text: 'text-orange-600', border: 'border-orange-200' };
    return { gradient: 'from-blue-500 to-teal-500', bg: 'bg-blue-50', text: 'text-blue-600', border: 'border-blue-200' };
  };

  const colors = getColorStyles(summary.title);

  return (
    <motion.div
      whileHover={{ y: -5, scale: 1.02 }}
      whileTap={{ scale: 0.98 }}
      onClick={onClick}
      className="relative group cursor-pointer"
    >
      {/* Background Decoration */}
      <div className={`absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r ${colors.gradient} rounded-2xl blur-xl opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-20 transition-opacity`}></div>
      
      {/* Main Card */}
      <div className="relative bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 overflow-hidden hover:shadow-xl transition-all duration-300">
        {/* Top Gradient Bar */}
        <div className={`h-2 bg-gradient-to-r ${colors.gradient}`}></div>
        
        <div className="p-6">
          {/* Header with Icon */}
          <div className="flex items-start gap-4 mb-4">
            <div className="relative">
              <div className={`absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r ${colors.gradient} rounded-xl blur-md opacity-30`}></div>
              <div className={`relative ${colors.bg} p-3 rounded-xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-300`}>
                <DocumentTextIcon className={`h-6 w-6 ${colors.text}`} />
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
              <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-800 group-hover:text-gray-900 transition line-clamp-1 text-lg">
                {summary.title}
              </h3>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <CalendarIcon className="h-3 w-3" />
                  {summary.date}
                </span>
                <span className="w-1 h-1 bg-gray-300 rounded-full"></span>
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <ClockIcon className="h-3 w-3" />
                  {summary.duration}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Preview Text */}
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4 line-clamp-2">
            {summary.preview}
          </p>

          {/* Topics */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
            {summary.topics.map((topic, i) => (
              <span 
                key={i} 
                className={`px-2 py-1 ${colors.bg} ${colors.text} text-xs rounded-lg border ${colors.border}`}
              >
                {topic}
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* View Link */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
            <span className="text-gray-400">Lecture Summary</span>
            <span className={`font-medium ${colors.text} flex items-center gap-1 group-hover:gap-2 transition-all`}>
              View Summary 
              <span className="text-lg">â†’</span>
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

const MySummaries = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [summaries, setSummaries] = useState([]);
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');
  const [hoveredFilter, setHoveredFilter] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate API call
    const fetchSummaries = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1500));
        setSummaries([
          {
            id: 1,
            title: 'Introduction to Machine Learning',
            date: '2024-02-24',
            duration: '45 min',
            topics: ['Supervised Learning', 'Neural Networks', 'AI'],
            preview: 'This lecture covers the fundamentals of machine learning, including supervised and unsupervised learning, neural networks basics, and real-world applications...'
          },
          {
            id: 2,
            title: 'Data Structures & Algorithms',
            date: '2024-02-23',
            duration: '60 min',
            topics: ['Arrays', 'Linked Lists', 'Trees', 'Graphs'],
            preview: 'Understanding basic data structures and their implementations in various programming languages with time complexity analysis...'
          },
          {
            id: 3,
            title: 'Database Management Systems',
            date: '2024-02-22',
            duration: '50 min',
            topics: ['SQL', 'Normalization', 'Transactions', 'Indexing'],
            preview: 'Deep dive into relational database design, SQL queries, transaction management, and query optimization techniques...'
          },
          {
            id: 4,
            title: 'Web Development Fundamentals',
            date: '2024-02-21',
            duration: '55 min',
            topics: ['HTML', 'CSS', 'JavaScript', 'React'],
            preview: 'Introduction to modern web development covering frontend technologies, responsive design, and building interactive user interfaces...'
          },
          {
            id: 5,
            title: 'Cloud Computing Basics',
            date: '2024-02-20',
            duration: '40 min',
            topics: ['AWS', 'Azure', 'GCP', 'DevOps'],
            preview: 'Overview of cloud service providers, their offerings, deployment models, and basic cloud architecture patterns...'
          },
          {
            id: 6,
            title: 'Cybersecurity Essentials',
            date: '2024-02-19',
            duration: '50 min',
            topics: ['Encryption', 'Network Security', 'Authentication'],
            preview: 'Fundamental concepts of cybersecurity including encryption algorithms, network security protocols, and authentication methods...'
          }
        ]);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching summaries:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchSummaries();
  }, []);

  const filteredSummaries = summaries.filter(summary => {
    const matchesSearch = summary.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||
                         summary.topics.some(topic => topic.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()));
    
    if (filter === 'all') return matchesSearch;
    if (filter === 'recent') {
      const sevenDaysAgo = new Date();
      sevenDaysAgo.setDate(sevenDaysAgo.getDate() - 7);
      return matchesSearch && new Date(summary.date) >= sevenDaysAgo;
    }
    return matchesSearch;
  });

  const containerVariants = {
    hidden: { opacity: 0 },
    visible: {
      opacity: 1,
      transition: {
        staggerChildren: 0.1
      }
    }
  };

  const itemVariants = {
    hidden: { y: 20, opacity: 0 },
    visible: {
      y: 0,
      opacity: 1,
      transition: {
        type: "spring",
        stiffness: 100,
        damping: 12
      }
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-[60vh] flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="relative">
          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-full blur-xl opacity-50 animate-pulse"></div>
          <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 p-6 rounded-full">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 border-4 border-white border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin"></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-50 via-white to-slate-50 py-8">
      {/* Animated Background Elements */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden pointer-events-none">
        <div className="absolute top-20 -left-4 w-72 h-72 bg-blue-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob"></div>
        <div className="absolute top-40 -right-4 w-72 h-72 bg-teal-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-2000"></div>
        <div className="absolute bottom-20 left-1/2 w-72 h-72 bg-purple-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-4000"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
        {/* Header Section - Styled like FileUploader */}
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          className="mb-10"
        >
          <div className="relative inline-block mb-4">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-2xl blur-xl opacity-30"></div>
            <div className="relative flex items-center gap-4 bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-sm rounded-2xl p-4 border-2 border-gray-100">
              <div className="relative">
                <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-xl blur-md opacity-50"></div>
                <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 p-3 rounded-xl">
                  <DocumentTextIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div>
                <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-teal-600 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
                  My Summaries
                </h1>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-1">
                  View and manage all your lecture summaries
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Search and Filter Section - Styled like FileUploader */}
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.1 }}
          className="mb-10"
        >
          <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-md">
            {/* Background Decoration */}
            <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
              <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-blue-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
              <div className="absolute -bottom-24 -left-24 w-48 h-48 bg-teal-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
            </div>

            <div className="relative flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4">
              {/* Search Input */}
              <div className="flex-1">
                <div className="relative group">
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-30 transition"></div>
                  <div className="relative flex items-center">
                    <MagnifyingGlassIcon className="absolute left-4 h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      placeholder="Search summaries by title or topic..."
                      value={searchTerm}
                      onChange={(e) => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}
                      className="w-full pl-12 pr-4 py-3 bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-lg focus:border-blue-400 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-200 transition outline-none text-gray-700 placeholder-gray-400"
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Filter and Clear */}
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <div className="relative group">
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-500 to-pink-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-30 transition"></div>
                  <select
                    value={filter}
                    onChange={(e) => setFilter(e.target.value)}
                    onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredFilter('select')}
                    onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredFilter(null)}
                    className="relative px-4 py-3 bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-lg focus:border-purple-400 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-purple-200 transition outline-none text-gray-700 appearance-none cursor-pointer pr-10"
                  >
                    <option value="all">All Time</option>
                    <option value="recent">Last 7 Days</option>
                  </select>
                  <FunnelIcon className="absolute right-3 top-3.5 h-5 w-5 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none" />
                </div>

                <motion.button
                  whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                  whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
                  onClick={() => {
                    setSearchTerm('');
                    setFilter('all');
                  }}
                  className="relative group"
                >
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-500 to-gray-600 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-30 transition"></div>
                  <div className="relative px-6 py-3 bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-lg font-medium text-gray-700 hover:border-gray-300 hover:shadow-md transition">
                    Clear
                  </div>
                </motion.button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Active Filters */}
            {(searchTerm || filter !== 'all') && (
              <motion.div 
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                className="mt-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-sm"
              >
                <span className="text-gray-500">Active filters:</span>
                {searchTerm && (
                  <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 rounded-full border border-blue-200">
                    Search: "{searchTerm}"
                  </span>
                )}
                {filter !== 'all' && (
                  <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-purple-50 text-purple-700 rounded-full border border-purple-200">
                    {filter === 'recent' ? 'Last 7 days' : filter}
                  </span>
                )}
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </div>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Results Count */}
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.2 }}
          className="mb-6 flex items-center justify-between"
        >
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">
            Showing <span className="font-semibold text-gray-700">{filteredSummaries.length}</span> of <span className="font-semibold text-gray-700">{summaries.length}</span> summaries
          </p>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <SparklesIcon className="h-4 w-4 text-yellow-500" />
            <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">AI-powered summaries</span>
          </div>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Summaries Grid */}
        {filteredSummaries.length > 0 ? (
          <motion.div 
            variants={containerVariants}
            initial="hidden"
            animate="visible"
            className="grid md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6"
          >
            {filteredSummaries.map((summary) => (
              <motion.div key={summary.id} variants={itemVariants}>
                <SummaryCard
                  summary={summary}
                  onClick={() => navigate(`/summary/${summary.id}`)}
                />
              </motion.div>
            ))}
          </motion.div>
        ) : (
          <motion.div 
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-12 shadow-md"
          >
            {/* Background Decoration */}
            <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
              <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-blue-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
              <div className="absolute -bottom-24 -left-24 w-48 h-48 bg-purple-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
            </div>

            <div className="relative text-center">
              <div className="flex justify-center mb-6">
                <div className="relative">
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-full blur-xl opacity-50"></div>
                  <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 p-5 rounded-full">
                    <DocumentTextIcon className="h-12 w-12 text-white" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <h3 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-3">No summaries found</h3>
              <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6 max-w-md mx-auto">
                {searchTerm || filter !== 'all' 
                  ? 'Try adjusting your search or filter to find what you\'re looking for' 
                  : 'Upload your first lecture to start generating AI-powered summaries'}
              </p>
              
              <motion.button
                whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
                onClick={() => navigate('/upload')}
                className="relative group inline-block"
              >
                <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-teal-600 rounded-lg blur-xl opacity-50 group-hover:opacity-70 transition"></div>
                <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-teal-600 text-white px-8 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-lg">+</span>
                  Upload Lecture
                </div>
              </motion.button>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </div>

      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes blob {
          0% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
          33% { transform: translate(30px, -50px) scale(1.1); }
          66% { transform: translate(-20px, 20px) scale(0.9); }
          100% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
        }
        .animate-blob {
          animation: blob 7s infinite;
        }
        .animation-delay-2000 {
          animation-delay: 2s;
        }
        .animation-delay-4000 {
          animation-delay: 4s;
        }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
};

export default MySummaries;

--- src\pages\Profile.jsx ---

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { UserCircleIcon, EnvelopeIcon, AcademicCapIcon, PencilIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import Button from '../components/common/Button';
import Input from '../components/common/Input';

const Profile = () => {
  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState(false);
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState({
    name: 'John Student',
    email: 'john.student@college.edu',
    course: 'B.Tech CSE',
    year: '3rd Year',
    college: 'CVR College of Engineering',
    bio: 'Computer Science student passionate about AI and Machine Learning. Always eager to learn new technologies.',
    stats: {
      totalSummaries: 47,
      totalTasks: 32,
      completedTasks: 28,
      hoursSaved: 156
    }
  });

  const [editedProfile, setEditedProfile] = useState({ ...profile });

  const handleSave = () => {
    setProfile(editedProfile);
    setIsEditing(false);
  };

  const handleCancel = () => {
    setEditedProfile({ ...profile });
    setIsEditing(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
      {/* Profile Header */}
      <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-primary-800 to-secondary-500 rounded-2xl p-8 text-white mb-8">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-6">
          <div className="h-24 w-24 bg-white rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <span className="text-4xl font-bold text-primary-800">
              {profile.name.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).join('')}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">{profile.name}</h1>
              {!isEditing ? (
                <Button
                  variant="secondary"
                  onClick={() => setIsEditing(true)}
                  className="flex items-center gap-2"
                >
                  <PencilIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                  Edit Profile
                </Button>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <Button variant="success" onClick={handleSave}>Save</Button>
                  <Button variant="outline" onClick={handleCancel}>Cancel</Button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            <p className="text-white/90 mt-1">{profile.course} â€¢ {profile.year}</p>
            <p className="text-white/80 text-sm mt-2">{profile.college}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Profile Content */}
      <div className="grid md:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
        {/* Left Column - Personal Info */}
        <div className="md:col-span-2 space-y-6">
          {/* About */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md p-6">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">About</h2>
            {isEditing ? (
              <textarea
                className="input-field min-h-[100px]"
                value={editedProfile.bio}
                onChange={(e) => setEditedProfile({ ...editedProfile, bio: e.target.value })}
              />
            ) : (
              <p className="text-gray-600">{profile.bio}</p>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Contact Info */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md p-6">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Contact Information</h2>
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <UserCircleIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                {isEditing ? (
                  <Input
                    value={editedProfile.name}
                    onChange={(e) => setEditedProfile({ ...editedProfile, name: e.target.value })}
                    className="flex-1"
                  />
                ) : (
                  <span className="text-gray-600">{profile.name}</span>
                )}
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <EnvelopeIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                {isEditing ? (
                  <Input
                    type="email"
                    value={editedProfile.email}
                    onChange={(e) => setEditedProfile({ ...editedProfile, email: e.target.value })}
                    className="flex-1"
                  />
                ) : (
                  <span className="text-gray-600">{profile.email}</span>
                )}
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <AcademicCapIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                {isEditing ? (
                  <div className="flex-1 flex gap-2">
                    <Input
                      value={editedProfile.course}
                      onChange={(e) => setEditedProfile({ ...editedProfile, course: e.target.value })}
                      className="flex-1"
                    />
                    <Input
                      value={editedProfile.year}
                      onChange={(e) => setEditedProfile({ ...editedProfile, year: e.target.value })}
                      className="w-32"
                    />
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <span className="text-gray-600">{profile.course} â€¢ {profile.year}</span>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Right Column - Stats */}
        <div className="space-y-6">
          {/* Statistics */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md p-6">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Statistics</h2>
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Total Summaries</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary-800">{profile.stats.totalSummaries}</p>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Total Tasks</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary-800">{profile.stats.totalTasks}</p>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Completed Tasks</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600">{profile.stats.completedTasks}</p>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Hours Saved</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-secondary-500">{profile.stats.hoursSaved}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Quick Actions */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md p-6">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Quick Actions</h2>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                className="w-full"
                onClick={() => navigate('/upload')}
              >
                Upload Lecture
              </Button>
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                className="w-full"
                onClick={() => navigate('/summaries')}
              >
                View Summaries
              </Button>
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                className="w-full"
                onClick={() => navigate('/tasks')}
              >
                View Tasks
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Profile;

--- src\pages\SavedNotes.jsx ---

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { BookmarkIcon, TrashIcon, PencilIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import Button from '../components/common/Button';
import Input from '../components/common/Input';
import Loader from '../components/common/Loader';

const SavedNotes = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState([]);
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate API call
    const fetchNotes = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1200));
        setNotes([
          {
            id: 1,
            title: 'Machine Learning Fundamentals',
            content: 'Key concepts from ML lecture: supervised learning, neural networks, backpropagation...',
            date: '2024-02-24',
            tags: ['ML', 'AI']
          },
          {
            id: 2,
            title: 'Data Structures Notes',
            content: 'Arrays: O(1) access, O(n) insertion. Linked Lists: O(n) access, O(1) insertion at head...',
            date: '2024-02-23',
            tags: ['DSA', 'Algorithms']
          },
          {
            id: 3,
            title: 'SQL Cheat Sheet',
            content: 'SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, JOIN types, GROUP BY, HAVING clauses...',
            date: '2024-02-22',
            tags: ['Database', 'SQL']
          }
        ]);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching notes:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchNotes();
  }, []);

  const filteredNotes = notes.filter(note =>
    note.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||
    note.content.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||
    note.tags.some(tag => tag.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()))
  );

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-[60vh] flex items-center justify-center">
        <Loader size="lg" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="mb-8">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900">Saved Notes</h1>
        <p className="text-gray-600 mt-2">
          Access your saved lecture notes and study materials
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* Search Bar */}
      <div className="mb-8">
        <Input
          type="text"
          placeholder="Search notes by title, content, or tags..."
          value={searchTerm}
          onChange={(e) => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}
        />
      </div>

      {/* Notes Grid */}
      {filteredNotes.length > 0 ? (
        <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {filteredNotes.map((note) => (
            <div
              key={note.id}
              className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow p-6"
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <BookmarkIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-primary-800" />
                  <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-900">{note.title}</h3>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <button className="text-gray-400 hover:text-primary-800">
                    <PencilIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </button>
                  <button className="text-gray-400 hover:text-red-600">
                    <TrashIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>

              <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-4 line-clamp-3">
                {note.content}
              </p>

              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
                {note.tags.map((tag, index) => (
                  <span
                    key={index}
                    className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary-50 text-primary-800 text-xs rounded-full"
                  >
                    {tag}
                  </span>
                ))}
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
                <span className="text-gray-500">{note.date}</span>
                <button
                  onClick={() => {/* View full note */}}
                  className="text-primary-800 hover:text-primary-900 font-medium"
                >
                  Read More â†’
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="text-center py-12">
          <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-full w-24 h-24 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
            <BookmarkIcon className="h-12 w-12 text-gray-400" />
          </div>
          <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-2">No notes found</h3>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6">
            {searchTerm ? 'Try adjusting your search' : 'Save summaries to access them here'}
          </p>
          <Button
            variant="primary"
            onClick={() => navigate('/summaries')}
          >
            Browse Summaries
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default SavedNotes;

--- src\pages\SummaryResults.jsx ---

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { summaryService } from '../services/summaryService';
import Loader from '../components/common/Loader';
import { ArrowLeftIcon, CalendarIcon, ClockIcon, TagIcon, BookOpenIcon, SparklesIcon, ExclamationCircleIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';

const SummaryResults = () => {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [summary, setSummary] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('summary');
  const [debugInfo, setDebugInfo] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchSummary = async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        setError(null);
        
        console.log('ðŸ” Fetching summary for lecture ID:', id);
        
        // Get all summaries
        const summariesResponse = await summaryService.getSummaries();
        console.log('ðŸ“¦ All summaries response:', summariesResponse);
        
        // Check the actual structure
        if (summariesResponse && summariesResponse.data) {
          console.log('ðŸ“Š Number of summaries:', summariesResponse.data.length);
          
          if (summariesResponse.data.length > 0) {
            // Log the first summary to see its structure
            const firstSummary = summariesResponse.data[0];
            console.log('ðŸ“ First summary structure:', {
              id: firstSummary.id,
              _id: firstSummary._id,
              lectureId: firstSummary.lectureId,
              allAvailableFields: Object.keys(firstSummary),
              sample: firstSummary
            });
            
            // Store debug info
            setDebugInfo({
              totalSummaries: summariesResponse.data.length,
              firstSummaryFields: Object.keys(firstSummary),
              lectureId: id
            });
            
            // Try multiple matching strategies
            const foundSummary = summariesResponse.data.find(s => {
              // Strategy 1: Check if any field contains the lecture ID
              const stringId = String(id);
              
              // Check all possible fields that might contain the lecture ID
              return (
                String(s._id) === stringId ||
                String(s.id) === stringId ||
                String(s.lectureId) === stringId ||
                String(s.lecture_id) === stringId ||
                String(s.fileId) === stringId ||
                String(s.uploadId) === stringId ||
                (s.title && String(s.title).includes(stringId)) ||
                // Check if any field value matches
                Object.values(s).some(val => 
                  val && String(val).includes(stringId)
                )
              );
            });
            
            if (foundSummary) {
              console.log('âœ… Summary found:', foundSummary);
              setSummary(foundSummary);
            } else {
              console.log('âŒ No summary found for lecture ID:', id);
              console.log('Available summaries:', summariesResponse.data.map(s => ({
                id: s._id || s.id,
                lectureId: s.lectureId,
                title: s.title
              })));
              setError('No summary found for this lecture. The summary may not have been generated yet.');
            }
          } else {
            setError('No summaries found in the system');
          }
        } else {
          setError('Invalid response structure from server');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('âŒ Error fetching summary:', error);
        setError(error.message || 'Failed to load summary');
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    if (id) {
      fetchSummary();
    }
  }, [id]);

  // Manual retry function
  const handleRetry = () => {
    setSummary(null);
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    setDebugInfo(null);
    
    setTimeout(() => {
      const fetchSummary = async () => {
        try {
          const summariesResponse = await summaryService.getSummaries();
          if (summariesResponse && summariesResponse.data) {
            const foundSummary = summariesResponse.data.find(s => {
              const stringId = String(id);
              return (
                String(s._id) === stringId ||
                String(s.id) === stringId ||
                String(s.lectureId) === stringId ||
                String(s.lecture_id) === stringId ||
                String(s.fileId) === stringId ||
                String(s.uploadId) === stringId ||
                Object.values(s).some(val => 
                  val && String(val).includes(stringId)
                )
              );
            });
            
            if (foundSummary) {
              setSummary(foundSummary);
            } else {
              setError('No summary found for this lecture. Please ensure the lecture has been processed.');
              setDebugInfo({
                totalSummaries: summariesResponse.data.length,
                lectureId: id
              });
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          setError(error.message || 'Failed to load summary');
        } finally {
          setLoading(false);
        }
      };
      
      fetchSummary();
    }, 100);
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center">
        <Loader size="lg" />
      </div>
    );
  }
  
  if (error || !summary) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-8 bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-50 via-white to-slate-50">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden pointer-events-none">
          <div className="absolute top-20 -left-4 w-72 h-72 bg-blue-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob"></div>
          <div className="absolute top-40 -right-4 w-72 h-72 bg-teal-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-2000"></div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="relative bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl p-12 max-w-md text-center">
          <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-red-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-6">
            <ExclamationCircleIcon className="h-12 w-12 text-red-600" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-3">Summary Not Found</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mb-4">
            {error || "We couldn't find a summary for this lecture. The lecture may still be processing or may have failed to generate."}
          </p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-6 bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded">
            Lecture ID: {id}
          </p>
          
          {/* Debug Info - Remove this in production */}
          {debugInfo && (
            <div className="mb-6 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg text-left text-xs">
              <p className="font-bold mb-2">Debug Info:</p>
              <p>Total summaries in system: {debugInfo.totalSummaries}</p>
              <p>Check browser console for more details</p>
            </div>
          )}
          
          <div className="flex gap-3 justify-center">
            <button
              onClick={handleRetry}
              className="bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-teal-600 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition transform hover:scale-105"
            >
              Try Again
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => navigate('/dashboard')}
              className="bg-gray-200 text-gray-700 px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold hover:bg-gray-300 transition"
            >
              Back to Dashboard
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Rest of your component remains exactly the same from here...
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-50 via-white to-slate-50">
      {/* Animated Background */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden pointer-events-none">
        <div className="absolute top-20 -left-4 w-72 h-72 bg-blue-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob"></div>
        <div className="absolute top-40 -right-4 w-72 h-72 bg-teal-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-2000"></div>
        <div className="absolute bottom-20 left-1/2 w-72 h-72 bg-purple-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-4000"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
        {/* Back Button */}
        <motion.button
          initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
          onClick={() => navigate('/dashboard')}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900 mb-6 group"
        >
          <ArrowLeftIcon className="h-4 w-4 group-hover:-translate-x-1 transition" />
          <span>Back to Dashboard</span>
        </motion.button>

        {/* Header */}
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          className="mb-8"
        >
          <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-teal-600 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            Lecture Summary
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mt-2">
            AI-generated summary and key insights from your lecture
          </p>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Tab Navigation */}
        {summary && (summary.content || summary.keyPoints?.length > 0 || summary.topics?.length > 0 || summary.transcript) && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            className="mb-6"
          >
            <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-1 shadow-md">
              <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
                <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-blue-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
              </div>
              <div className="relative flex gap-1">
                {[
                  { id: 'summary', label: 'Summary', icon: BookOpenIcon, condition: summary.content },
                  { id: 'keypoints', label: 'Key Points', icon: SparklesIcon, condition: summary.keyPoints?.length > 0 },
                  { id: 'topics', label: 'Topics', icon: TagIcon, condition: summary.topics?.length > 0 },
                  { id: 'transcript', label: 'Transcript', icon: ClockIcon, condition: summary.transcript }
                ].filter(tab => tab.condition).map((tab) => (
                  <button
                    key={tab.id}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}
                    className={`
                      flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg font-medium capitalize transition-all
                      ${activeTab === tab.id
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 text-white shadow-md'
                        : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50'
                      }
                    `}
                  >
                    <tab.icon className="h-4 w-4" />
                    {tab.label}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}

        {/* Content Area */}
        {summary && (
          <motion.div
            key={activeTab}
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
            className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-xl border border-gray-200 p-8"
          >
            {/* Summary Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'summary' && (
              <div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                  <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 p-2 rounded-lg">
                    <BookOpenIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800">AI-Generated Summary</h2>
                </div>
                <div className="prose max-w-none">
                  <p className="text-gray-700 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-line text-lg">
                    {summary.content || "No summary available."}
                  </p>
                </div>
                {summary.confidence && (
                  <div className="mt-6 p-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-50 to-teal-50 rounded-lg border border-blue-100">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <span className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">AI Confidence Score</span>
                      <span className="text-sm font-bold text-blue-600">{summary.confidence}%</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-2 h-2 bg-gray-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                      <div 
                        className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-full"
                        style={{ width: `${summary.confidence}%` }}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Key Points Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'keypoints' && summary.keyPoints?.length > 0 && (
              <div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                  <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 p-2 rounded-lg">
                    <SparklesIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800">Key Points</h2>
                </div>
                <ul className="space-y-4">
                  {summary.keyPoints.map((point, index) => (
                    <motion.li
                      key={index}
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                      transition={{ delay: index * 0.1 }}
                      className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-50 to-transparent rounded-lg border border-orange-100"
                    >
                      <span className="flex-shrink-0 w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 text-white rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-sm font-bold shadow-md">
                        {index + 1}
                      </span>
                      <p className="text-gray-700 flex-1">{point}</p>
                    </motion.li>
                  ))}
                </ul>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Topics Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'topics' && summary.topics?.length > 0 && (
              <div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                  <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-500 to-pink-500 p-2 rounded-lg">
                    <TagIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800">Topics Covered</h2>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
                  {summary.topics.map((topic, index) => (
                    <motion.span
                      key={index}
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
                      transition={{ delay: index * 0.05 }}
                      className="px-4 py-2 bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-100 to-pink-100 text-gray-800 rounded-full text-sm font-medium border border-purple-200 shadow-sm"
                    >
                      {topic}
                    </motion.span>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Transcript Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'transcript' && summary.transcript && (
              <div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                  <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-teal-500 to-emerald-500 p-2 rounded-lg">
                    <ClockIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800">Full Transcript</h2>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-6 max-h-96 overflow-y-auto border border-gray-200">
                  <p className="text-gray-700 whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm leading-relaxed">
                    {summary.transcript}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </motion.div>
        )}

        {/* Footer with Metadata */}
        {summary && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            transition={{ delay: 0.3 }}
            className="mt-8 grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4"
          >
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="bg-blue-50 p-2 rounded-lg">
                  <CalendarIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Created</p>
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800">
                    {summary.createdAt ? new Date(summary.createdAt).toLocaleDateString() : 'N/A'}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="bg-green-50 p-2 rounded-lg">
                  <TagIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-green-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Topics</p>
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800">
                    {summary.topics?.length || 0} topics
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="bg-purple-50 p-2 rounded-lg">
                  <SparklesIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Key Points</p>
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800">
                    {summary.keyPoints?.length || 0} points
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="bg-orange-50 p-2 rounded-lg">
                  <ClockIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-orange-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Confidence</p>
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800">
                    {summary.confidence || 0}%
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </div>

      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes blob {
          0% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
          33% { transform: translate(30px, -50px) scale(1.1); }
          66% { transform: translate(-20px, 20px) scale(0.9); }
          100% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
        }
        .animate-blob {
          animation: blob 7s infinite;
        }
        .animation-delay-2000 {
          animation-delay: 2s;
        }
        .animation-delay-4000 {
          animation-delay: 4s;
        }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SummaryResults;

--- src\pages\TaskDetails.jsx ---

  CheckCircleIcon,
  ExclamationCircleIcon,

            instructor: 'Prof. Michael Chen',

            longDescription: 'Chapter 5 covers the mathematics of backpropagation, various optimization algorithms (SGD, Momentum, Adam), and regularization techniques. Focus on understanding the chain rule application in backpropagation and the differences between optimization algorithms.\n\nTake comprehensive notes that you can use as reference for future assignments and exams. Pay special attention to the derivation of gradients and the intuition behind each optimization method.',
            deadline: '2024-02-28',
            priority: 'Medium',
            status: 'in-progress',
            progress: 30,
            created: '2024-02-19',
            estimatedHours: 4,
            resources: [
              { name: 'Chapter 5 PDF', type: 'pdf', size: '8.7 MB' },
              { name: 'Supplementary Notes', type: 'pdf', size: '1.2 MB' }
            ],
            subtasks: [
              { id: 1, title: 'Read sections 5.1-5.3', completed: true },
              { id: 2, title: 'Take notes on backpropagation', completed: true },
              { id: 3, title: 'Read sections 5.4-5.6', completed: false },
              { id: 4, title: 'Summarize optimization algorithms', completed: false }
            ],
            comments: [],
            attachments: []
          }
        };

        setTask(mockTasks[id] || mockTasks[1]);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching task:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchTask();
  }, [id]);

  const getPriorityStyles = (priority) => {
    switch(priority) {
      case 'High':
        return {
          badge: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-red-500 to-pink-500 text-white',
          progress: 'from-red-500 to-pink-500',
          icon: <ExclamationCircleIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-red-500" />,
          bg: 'bg-red-50',
          border: 'border-red-200',
          text: 'text-red-700',
          light: 'bg-red-50/50'
        };
      case 'Medium':
        return {
          badge: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-yellow-500 to-orange-500 text-white',
          progress: 'from-yellow-500 to-orange-500',
          icon: <ClockIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-500" />,
          bg: 'bg-yellow-50',
          border: 'border-yellow-200',
          text: 'text-yellow-700',
          light: 'bg-yellow-50/50'
        };
      case 'Low':
        return {
          badge: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 to-teal-500 text-white',
          progress: 'from-green-500 to-teal-500',
          icon: <CheckCircleIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-green-500" />,
          bg: 'bg-green-50',
          border: 'border-green-200',
          text: 'text-green-700',
          light: 'bg-green-50/50'
        };
      default:
        return {
          badge: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-500 to-gray-600 text-white',
          progress: 'from-gray-500 to-gray-600',
          icon: <ClockIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-500" />,
          bg: 'bg-gray-50',
          border: 'border-gray-200',
          text: 'text-gray-700',
          light: 'bg-gray-50/50'
        };
    }
  };

  const getStatusStyles = (status) => {
    switch(status) {
      case 'completed':
        return 'bg-green-100 text-green-700 border-green-200';
      case 'in-progress':
        return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 border-blue-200';
      default:
        return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 border-gray-200';
    }
  };

  const getDaysLeft = (deadline) => {
    const today = new Date();
    const dueDate = new Date(deadline);
    const diffTime = dueDate - today;
    const diffDays = Math.ceil(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    return diffDays;
  };

  const containerVariants = {
    hidden: { opacity: 0 },
    visible: {
      opacity: 1,
      transition: {
        staggerChildren: 0.1
      }
    }
  };

  const itemVariants = {
    hidden: { y: 20, opacity: 0 },
    visible: {
      y: 0,
      opacity: 1,
      transition: {
        type: "spring",
        stiffness: 100,
        damping: 12
      }
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-50 via-white to-slate-50 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="relative">
          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 rounded-full blur-xl opacity-50 animate-pulse"></div>
          <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 p-6 rounded-full">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 border-4 border-white border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin"></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const priority = getPriorityStyles(task?.priority);
  const daysLeft = getDaysLeft(task?.deadline);
  const isOverdue = daysLeft < 0;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-50 via-white to-slate-50 py-8">
      {/* Animated Background Elements */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden pointer-events-none">
        <div className="absolute top-20 -left-4 w-72 h-72 bg-orange-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob"></div>
        <div className="absolute top-40 -right-4 w-72 h-72 bg-red-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-2000"></div>
        <div className="absolute bottom-20 left-1/2 w-72 h-72 bg-yellow-300 rounded-full mix-blend-multiply filter blur-xl opacity-20 animate-blob animation-delay-4000"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
        {/* Back Button */}
        <motion.button
          initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
          onClick={() => navigate('/tasks')}
          className="relative group mb-6 inline-flex items-center gap-2"
        >
          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-500 to-gray-600 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-30 transition"></div>
          <div className="relative flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-lg hover:border-gray-300 transition">
            <ArrowLeftIcon className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-600" />
            <span className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">Back to Tasks</span>
          </div>
        </motion.button>

        {/* Header Section */}
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}

          className="mb-8"
        >

            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 rounded-2xl blur-xl opacity-30"></div>
            <div className="relative bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-sm rounded-2xl p-6 border-2 border-gray-100">
              <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center md:justify-between gap-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                  <div className="relative">
                    <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 rounded-xl blur-md opacity-50"></div>

                      {priority.icon}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-600 to-red-600 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
                      {task?.title}
                    </h1>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mt-2 text-sm text-gray-500">
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <UserIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                        {task?.instructor}
                      </span>
                      <span className="w-1 h-1 bg-gray-300 rounded-full"></span>
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <TagIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                        {task?.course}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <span className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-medium border ${getStatusStyles(task?.status)}`}>
                    {task?.status}
                  </span>
                  <span className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-medium ${priority.badge}`}>
                    {task?.priority} Priority
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Tab Navigation */}
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.1 }}
          className="mb-6"
        >
          <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-1 shadow-md">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
              <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-orange-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
            </div>
            <div className="relative flex gap-1">
              {['overview', 'subtasks', 'resources', 'comments'].map((tab) => (
                <button
                  key={tab}
                  onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab)}
                  className={`
                    flex-1 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg font-medium capitalize transition-all
                    ${activeTab === tab
                      ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 text-white shadow-md'
                      : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50'
                    }
                  `}
                >
                  {tab}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Content Grid */}
        <div className="grid lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {/* Main Content - 2 columns */}
          <motion.div 
            variants={containerVariants}
            initial="hidden"
            animate="visible"
            className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-6"
          >
            {/* Overview Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'overview' && (
              <motion.div variants={itemVariants}>
                <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-8 shadow-md">
                  {/* Background Decoration */}
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
                    <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-orange-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
                    <div className="absolute -bottom-24 -left-24 w-48 h-48 bg-red-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="relative">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                      <div className="relative">
                        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-red-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-30"></div>
                        <div className={`relative ${priority.bg} p-2 rounded-lg`}>
                          <DocumentTextIcon className={`h-5 w-5 ${priority.text}`} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">Description</h2>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="prose max-w-none">
                      <p className="text-gray-700 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-line">
                        {task?.longDescription || task?.description}
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    {/* Progress Section */}
                    <div className="mt-8 p-6 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-100">
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                        <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-800">Progress</h3>
                        <span className={`text-sm font-medium ${priority.text}`}>{task?.progress}% Complete</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="h-3 bg-gray-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div 
                          className={`h-full rounded-full bg-gradient-to-r ${priority.progress}`}

                      </div>
                      <div className="flex justify-between mt-4 text-sm">
                        <span className="text-gray-500">Started: {task?.created}</span>

                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            )}

            {/* Subtasks Tab */}
            {activeTab === 'subtasks' && (
              <motion.div variants={itemVariants}>
                <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-8 shadow-md">
                  <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-5">
                    <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-yellow-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="relative">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                      <div className="relative">
                        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-yellow-500 to-orange-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-30"></div>

                          <CheckCircleIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-white" />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">Subtasks</h2>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="space-y-3">
                      {task?.subtasks.map((subtask) => (
                        <div 
                          key={subtask.id}
                          className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-100 hover:border-orange-200 transition"
                        >
                          <input
                            type="checkbox"
                            checked={subtask.completed}
                            readOnly
                            className="w-5 h-5 text-orange-500 rounded border-gray-300"
                          />
                          <span className={`flex-1 ${subtask.completed ? 'text-gray-400 line-through' : 'text-gray-700'}`}>
                            {subtask.title}
                          </span>
                          {subtask.completed && (

                  </div>
                </div>
              </motion.div>

            {activeTab === 'resources' && (

                      <div className="relative">
                        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-500 to-pink-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-30"></div>

                          <PaperClipIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-white" />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">Resources</h2>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="space-y-3">
                      {task?.resources.map((resource, index) => (
                        <div 
                          key={index}
                          className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-100 hover:border-purple-200 transition"
                        >
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                            <div className="p-2 bg-purple-100 rounded-lg">
                              <DocumentTextIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-600" />
                            </div>
                            <div>
                              <p className="font-medium text-gray-800">{resource.name}</p>
                              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{resource.type.toUpperCase()} â€¢ {resource.size}</p>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          <button className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-purple-600 text-white text-sm rounded-lg hover:bg-purple-700 transition">
                            Download
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>

                    {task?.attachments.length > 0 && (
                      <>
                        <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-800 mt-8 mb-4">Your Attachments</h3>
                        <div className="space-y-3">
                          {task?.attachments.map((attachment, index) => (
                            <div 
                              key={index}
                              className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 bg-blue-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-blue-100"
                            >
                              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                                <div className="p-2 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg">
                                  <DocumentTextIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                                </div>
                                <div>
                                  <p className="font-medium text-gray-800">{attachment.name}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{attachment.size} â€¢ Uploaded {attachment.uploaded}</p>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <span className="text-xs px-2 py-1 bg-green-100 text-green-700 rounded-full">
                                Submitted
                              </span>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </>

            {/* Comments Tab */}

                    <div className="absolute -top-24 -right-24 w-48 h-48 bg-blue-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="relative">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                      <div className="relative">
                        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-lg blur-md opacity-30"></div>
                        <div className="relative bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 p-2 rounded-lg">
                          <ChatBubbleLeftIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-white" />

                      </div>

                    {/* Comments List */}

            )}
          </motion.div>

          {/* Sidebar - 1 column */}
          <motion.div 
            variants={containerVariants}

              <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-md">

                  <div className="absolute -bottom-24 -left-24 w-48 h-48 bg-orange-500 rounded-full blur-3xl"></div>

                  <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-4">Task Information</h3>

                    <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                      <span className="text-sm text-gray-500">Status</span>
                      <span className={`text-sm px-3 py-1 rounded-full border ${getStatusStyles(task?.status)}`}>

                        </span>
                        <span className={`text-xs ${isOverdue ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-gray-400'}`}>

                      </div>

                        />

                    </div>

                      <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div 
                          className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-500 to-teal-500 rounded-full"
                          style={{ width: `${(task?.subtasks.filter(s => s.completed).length / task?.subtasks.length) * 100}%` }}
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          </motion.div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes blob {
          0% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
          33% { transform: translate(30px, -50px) scale(1.1); }
          66% { transform: translate(-20px, 20px) scale(0.9); }
          100% { transform: translate(0px, 0px) scale(1); }
        }
        .animate-blob {
          animation: blob 7s infinite;
        }
        .animation-delay-2000 {
          animation-delay: 2s;
        }
        .animation-delay-4000 {
          animation-delay: 4s;
        }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
};

export default TaskDetails;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { 
  CalendarIcon,
  ClockIcon,
  CheckCircleIcon,
  ExclamationCircleIcon,
  SparklesIcon,
  FunnelIcon,
  MagnifyingGlassIcon,
  ArrowPathIcon
} from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';

const TasksPage = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState([]);
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
  const [hoveredTask, setHoveredTask] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate API call
    const fetchTasks = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1500));
        setTasks([
          {
            id: 1,

            progress: 30,
            created: '2024-02-19'
          },
          {

            description: 'Submit the final project proposal document including problem statement, methodology, and timeline.',
            deadline: '2024-03-05',

            progress: 90,
            created: '2024-02-18'
          },
          {
